Data Structures and Algorithms with Python

11. B-Trees¶

This chapter covers one of the more important data structures of the last thirty years. B-Trees are primarily used by relational databases to efficiently implement an operation called join. B-Trees have other properties that are also useful for databases including ordering of rows within a table, fast delete capability, and sequential access. The chapter begins by introducing some terminology from relational databases to motivate the need for B-Trees. It goes on to introduce the B-Tree data structure and its implementation. By the end of this chapter you should have an understanding of B-Trees, their advantages over other data structures, and you should be able to demonstrate your understanding by implementing a B-Tree that can be used to efficiently process joins in relational databases.

11.1. Relational Database Tables¶

You can find the three database tables from the text here.

  • Feed.tbl

  • FeedAttribute.tbl

  • FeedAttribType.tbl

11.2. The Inefficient Join Program¶

The inefficient join program can be downloaded by clicking here.

  1import datetime
  2
  3def readField(record,colTypes,fieldNum):
  4    # fieldNum is zero based
  5    # record is a string containing the record
  6    # colTypes is the types for each of the columns in the record
  7    
  8    offset = 0
  9    for i in range(fieldNum):
 10        colType = colTypes[i]
 11        
 12        if colType == "int":
 13            offset+=10
 14        elif colType[:4] == "char":
 15            size = int(colType[4:])
 16            offset += size
 17        elif colType == "float":
 18            offset+=20
 19        elif colType == "datetime":
 20            offset+=24
 21            
 22    colType = colTypes[fieldNum]
 23   
 24    if colType == "int":
 25        value = record[offset:offset+10].strip()
 26        if value == "null":
 27            val = None
 28        else:
 29            val = int(value)
 30    elif colType == "float":
 31        value = record[offset:offset+20].strip()
 32        if value == "null":
 33            val = None
 34        else:        
 35            val = float(value)
 36    elif colType[:4] == "char":
 37        size = int(colType[4:])
 38        value = record[offset:offset+size].strip()
 39        if value == "null":
 40            val = None
 41        else:   
 42            val = value[1:-1] # remove the ' and ' from each end of the string
 43            if type(val) == bytes:
 44                val = val.decode("utf-8")
 45    elif colType == "datetime":
 46        value = record[offset:offset+24].strip()
 47        if value == "null":
 48            val = None
 49        else:
 50            if type(val) == bytes:
 51                val = val.decode("utf-8") 
 52            val = datetime.datetime.strptime(val,'%m/%d/%Y %I:%M:%S %p')
 53    else:
 54        print("Unrecognized Type")
 55        raise Exception("Unrecognized Type") 
 56    
 57    return val         
 58
 59def main():
 60    # SELECT Feed.FeedNum, Feed.Name, FeedAttribType.Name, FeedAttribute.Value WHERE
 61    # Feed.FeedID = FeedAttribute.FeedID AND 
 62    # FeedAttribute.FeedAttribTypeID = FeedAttribType.FeedAttribTypeID
 63    
 64    attribTypeCols = ["int","char20","char60","int","int","int","int"]
 65    feedCols = ["int","int","int","char50","datetime","float","float","int","char50","int"]
 66    feedAttributeCols = ["int","int","float"]
 67    
 68    before = datetime.datetime.now()
 69    feedAttributeTable = open("FeedAttribute.tbl","r")
 70    
 71    for record in feedAttributeTable:
 72        
 73        feedID = readField(record,feedAttributeCols,0)
 74        feedAttribTypeID = readField(record,feedAttributeCols,1)
 75        value = readField(record,feedAttributeCols,2)
 76        
 77        feedTable = open("Feed.tbl","r")
 78        
 79        feedFeedID = -1
 80        
 81        while feedFeedID != feedID:
 82            feedRecord = feedTable.readline()   
 83            feedFeedID = readField(feedRecord,feedCols,0)
 84            
 85            
 86        feedNum = readField(feedRecord,feedCols,2)
 87        feedName = readField(feedRecord,feedCols,3)
 88        
 89        feedAttribTypeTable = open("FeedAttribType.tbl", "r")
 90        
 91        feedAttribTypeIDID = -1
 92        
 93        while feedAttribTypeIDID != feedAttribTypeID:
 94            feedAttribTypeRecord = feedAttribTypeTable.readline()
 95            feedAttribTypeIDID = readField(feedAttribTypeRecord,attribTypeCols,0)
 96            
 97        feedAttribTypeName = readField(feedAttribTypeRecord,attribTypeCols,1)
 98        
 99        print(feedNum,feedName,feedAttribTypeName,value)
100    after = datetime.datetime.now()
101    deltaT = after - before
102    milliseconds = deltaT.total_seconds() * 1000    
103    print("Done. The total time for the query without indexing was",milliseconds, \
104        "milliseconds.")
105    
106if __name__ == "__main__":
107    main()

11.3. B-Tree Implementations¶

B-Trees, like most other tree data structures can be implemented both iteratively and recursively. Both implementations are described in the text and they both have starter shells provided here.

Each implementation includes two main functions. The btreemain in each contains a test program. Sample output is included in the file for the btreemain function. The other main function contains the join query using the B-Tree implementation to construct a B-Tree index over two of the database tables to improve the join efficiency. Comparing either of these queries to the inefficient join program above will illustrate the advantage of a B-Tree over sequential search.

11.3.1. Iterative B-Tree¶

This shell is provided as an implementation that supports an iterative implementation of insert, delete, and update. The starting shell can be downloaded here. As stated above, the program contains two main functions for testing of the B-Tree implementation. The Stack implementation is required for this program and can be downloaded here. The Queue implementation is required for this program and can be downloaded here. These two files must be placed in the same directory as the database tables and the B-Tree implementation file.

  1'''
  2  File: btree.py
  3  Author: Steve Hubbard and Kent D. Lee
  4  Date: 8/27/2014
  5  Description: This module provides the BTree class, based on support from
  6    the BTreeNode class.  The BTreeNode class is also implemented in this 
  7    module. This module is meant to support the iterative implementation of 
  8    insert and lookup within a BTree. 
  9
 10    The module requires the Stack and Queue classes from the corresponding
 11    two modules, stack.py and queue.py. 
 12
 13    This program has two main functions, the btreemain function and the main
 14    function. The btreemain function tests the BTree datatype. The expected
 15    output is provided in a comment after the function. Once the btreemain 
 16    function runs and produces the proper output, the main function can be 
 17    run to test the BTree with the join functionality. 
 18
 19    The main function either builds a new BTree or reads an existing BTree 
 20    from the index files, Feed.idx and FeedAttribType.idx files. If the idx
 21    file does not exist, then a new BTree is built and written to the 
 22    corresponding idx file. 
 23'''
 24
 25import datetime
 26import os
 27from copy import deepcopy
 28import sys
 29import stack
 30import queue
 31
 32
 33class BTreeNode:
 34    '''
 35      This module provides the BTreeNode class.  This class will
 36      be used by the BTree class.  Much of the functionality of
 37      B-trees is provided by this class.
 38    '''    
 39    def __init__(self, degree = 1, numberOfKeys = 0, items = None, child = None, \
 40        index = None):
 41        ''' Create an empty node with the indicated degree'''
 42        self.numberOfKeys = numberOfKeys
 43        if items != None:
 44            self.items = items
 45        else:
 46            self.items = [None]*2*degree
 47        if child != None:
 48            self.child = child
 49        else:
 50            self.child = [None]*(2*degree+1)
 51        self.index = index
 52
 53    def __repr__(self):
 54        return "BTreeNode("+str(len(self.items)//2)+","+str(self.numberOfKeys)+ \
 55            ","+repr(self.items)+","+repr(self.child)+","+str(self.index)+")\n"
 56
 57    def __str__(self):
 58        st = 'The contents of the node with index '+ \
 59             str(self.index) + ':\n'
 60        for i in range(0, self.numberOfKeys):
 61            st += '   Index   ' + str(i) + '  >  child: '
 62            st += str(self.child[i])
 63            st += '   item: '
 64            st += str(self.items[i]) + '\n'
 65        st += '                 child: '
 66        st += str(self.child[self.numberOfKeys]) + '\n'
 67        return st
 68
 69    def addItemAndSplit(self, anItem, left, right):
 70        ''' 
 71         If the receiver is not full, generate an error.
 72         If full, split the receiver into two nodes, the
 73         smallest degree + 1 keys staying in the original node.
 74         The largest degree keys go into a new node which is
 75         returned. Note that the last child of the receiver
 76         and the first child of the new node will be the same.
 77        '''
 78        pass
 79
 80    def getChild(self,i):
 81        # Answer the index of the ith child
 82        if (0 <= i <= self.numberOfKeys):
 83            return self.child[i]
 84        else:
 85            print( 'Error in getChild().' )
 86            
 87    def setChild(self, i, childIndex):
 88        # Set the ith child of the node to childIndex
 89        self.child[i] = childIndex
 90
 91    def childIndexOf(self, anIndex):
 92        # Answer the index of the child in the receiver
 93        # which contains anIndex.
 94        index = -1
 95        k = 0
 96        found = False
 97        while not found and k <= self.numberOfKeys :
 98            if self.child[k] == anIndex:
 99                index = k
100                found = True
101            else:
102                k += 1
103        if index < 0:
104            print( 'Error in childIndexOf' )
105            return -1
106        else:
107            return index
108
109    def clear(self):
110        self.numberOfKeys = 0
111        self.items = [None]*len(self.items)
112        self.child = [None]*len(self.child)
113    
114    def copyItemsAndChildren(self, fromNode, start,
115                             finish, index):
116        '''The receiver gets the contents of the fromNode from
117          index start to finish, along with the next child.
118          The copying within the receiver begins at position
119          index. Answer the receiver.
120        '''
121        pass
122  
123    def copyWithRight(self, aNode, parentNode):  
124        '''Answer a node which contains all the items and children
125          of the receiver, followed by the parent item followed by
126          all the items and children of aNode.  The receiver and
127          aNode are left and right siblings wrt the parentNode.
128        '''
129        pass
130    
131    def insertItem(self, anItem, left, right):  
132        ''' We assume that the receiver is not full. anItem is
133          inserted into the BTreeNode with child indices left and
134          right.  This is done while retaining the <= ordering on
135          the key of the item.  If the insertion is successful,
136          answer True.  If not, answer False.
137        '''
138        pass
139
140    def isFull(self):
141        ''' Answer True if the receiver is full.  If not, return
142          False.
143        '''
144        return (self.numberOfKeys == len(self.items))
145
146    def removeChild(self, index):
147        ''' If the index is valid, remove and answer the child at
148          location index.  If not, answer None.  In any event,
149          do NOT update the key count.  We copy all the rest of
150          the child entries down one, as removeItem will
151          decrement numberOfKeys.
152        '''
153        pass
154
155    def removeItem(self, index):
156        '''If index is valid, remove and answer the item at
157          location index. Update the key count.  If not, answer
158          None.
159        '''
160        pass
161
162    def searchNode(self, anItem):
163        '''Answer a dictionary satisfying: at 'found'
164          either True or False depending upon whether the receiver
165          has a matching item;  at 'nodeIndex', either the index of
166          the matching item, or in the case of an unsuccessful
167          search, the index of the smallest (first) item such that
168          anItem < item, or self.numberOfKeys if all items
169          are < anItem.  In other words, nodeIndex is the place in the node
170          where the object is, or should go if there is room in the node.
171        '''
172        pass       
173
174    def setIndex(self, anInteger):
175        self.index = anInteger
176
177    def setNumberOfKeys(self, anInt ):
178        self.numberOfKeys = anInt
179
180class BTree:
181    def __init__(self, degree, nodes = {}, rootIndex = 1, freeIndex = 2):
182        # This method is complete
183        self.degree = degree
184        
185        if len(nodes) == 0:
186            self.rootNode = BTreeNode(degree)
187            self.nodes = {}
188            self.rootNode.setIndex(rootIndex)
189            self.writeAt(1, self.rootNode)  
190        else:
191            self.nodes = deepcopy(nodes)
192            self.rootNode = self.nodes[rootIndex]   
193            
194        self.stackOfNodes = stack.Stack()   
195        self.rootIndex = rootIndex
196        self.freeIndex = freeIndex
197        
198    def __repr__(self):
199        # This method is complete
200        return "BTree("+str(self.degree)+",\n "+repr(self.nodes)+","+ \
201            str(self.rootIndex)+","+str(self.freeIndex)+")"
202
203    def __str__(self):
204        # This method is complete 
205        st = '  The degree of the BTree is ' + str(self.degree)+\
206             '.\n'
207        st += '  The index of the root node is ' + \
208              str(self.rootIndex) + '.\n'
209        for x in range(1, self.freeIndex):
210            node = self.readFrom(x)
211            if node.getNumberOfKeys() > 0:
212                st += str(node) 
213        return st
214
215          
216    def delete(self, anItem):
217        ''' Answer None if a matching item is not found.  If found,
218          answer the entire item.  
219        '''
220        pass
221
222    def getFreeIndex(self):
223        # Answer a new index and update freeIndex.  Private
224        self.freeIndex += 1
225        return self.freeIndex - 1
226
227    def getFreeNode(self):
228        #Answer a new BTreeNode with its index set correctly.
229        #Also, update freeIndex.  Private
230        newNode = BTreeNode(self.degree)
231        index = self.getFreeIndex()
232        newNode.setIndex(index)
233        self.writeAt(index,newNode)
234        return newNode
235
236    def inorderOn(self, aFile):
237        '''
238          Print the items of the BTree in inorder on the file 
239          aFile.  aFile is open for writing.
240          This method is complete at this time. 
241        '''
242        aFile.write("An inorder traversal of the BTree:\n")
243        self.inorderOnFrom( aFile, self.rootIndex)
244
245    def inorderOnFrom(self, aFile, index):
246        ''' Print the items of the subtree of the BTree, which is
247          rooted at index, in inorder on aFile.
248        '''
249        pass
250
251    def insert(self, anItem):
252        ''' Answer None if the BTree already contains a matching
253          item. If not, insert a deep copy of anItem and answer
254          anItem.
255        '''
256        pass
257
258    def levelByLevel(self, aFile):
259        ''' Print the nodes of the BTree level-by-level on aFile. )
260        '''
261        pass
262
263    def readFrom(self, index):
264        ''' Answer the node at entry index of the btree structure.
265          Later adapt to files
266        '''
267        if self.nodes.__contains__(index):
268            return self.nodes[index]
269        else:
270            return None
271
272    def recycle(self, aNode):
273        # For now, do nothing
274        aNode.clear()
275
276    def retrieve(self, anItem):
277        ''' If found, answer a deep copy of the matching item.
278          If not found, answer None
279        '''
280        pass  
281
282    def __searchTree(self, anItem):
283        ''' Answer a dictionary.  If there is a matching item, at
284          'found' is True, at 'fileIndex' is the index of the node
285          in the BTree with the matching item, and at 'nodeIndex'
286          is the index into the node of the matching item.  If not,
287          at 'found' is False, but the entry for 'fileIndex' is the
288          leaf node where the search terminated.  An important
289          function of this method is that it pushes all of the
290          nodes of the search path from the rootnode, down to,
291          but not including the corresponding leaf node of a search
292          (or the node containing a match).  Again, the rootnode
293          is pushed if it is not a leaf node and has no match.
294        '''
295        pass
296
297    def update(self, anItem):
298        ''' If found, update the item with a matching key to be a
299          deep copy of anItem and answer anItem.  If not, answer None.
300        '''
301        pass
302
303    def writeAt(self, index, aNode):
304        ''' Set the element in the btree with the given index
305          to aNode.  This method must be invoked to make any
306          permanent changes to the btree.  We may later change
307          this method to work with files.
308          This method is complete at this time.
309        '''
310        self.nodes[index] = aNode
311
312def btreemain():
313    print("My/Our name(s) is/are ")
314
315    lst = [10,8,22,14,12,18,2,50,15]
316    
317    b = BTree(2)
318    
319    for x in lst:
320        print(repr(b))
321        print("***Inserting",x)
322        b.insert(x)
323    
324    print(repr(b))
325    
326    lst = [14,50,8,12,18,2,10,22,15]
327    
328    for x in lst:
329        print("***Deleting",x)
330        b.delete(x) 
331        print(repr(b))
332    
333    #return 
334    lst = [54,76]
335    
336    for x in lst:
337        print("***Deleting",x)
338        b.delete(x)
339        print(repr(b))
340        
341    print("***Inserting 14")    
342    b.insert(14)
343    
344    print(repr(b))
345    
346    print("***Deleting 2")
347    b.delete(2)
348    
349    print(repr(b))
350    
351    print ("***Deleting 84")
352    b.delete(84)
353    
354    print(repr(b))
355
356    return

476},1,5)
477***Deleting 54
478BTree(2,
479 {1: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],1)
480, 2: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],2)
481, 3: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],3)
482, 4: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],4)
483},1,5)
484***Deleting 76
485BTree(2,
486 {1: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],1)
487, 2: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],2)
488, 3: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],3)
489, 4: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],4)
490},1,5)
491***Inserting 14
492BTree(2,
493 {1: BTreeNode(2,1,[14, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],1)
494, 2: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],2)
495, 3: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],3)
496, 4: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],4)
497},1,5)
498***Deleting 2
499BTree(2,
500 {1: BTreeNode(2,1,[14, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],1)
501, 2: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],2)
502, 3: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],3)
503, 4: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],4)
504},1,5)
505***Deleting 84
506BTree(2,
507 {1: BTreeNode(2,1,[14, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],1)
508, 2: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],2)
509, 3: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],3)
510, 4: BTreeNode(2,0,[None, None, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],4)
511},1,5)
512'''
513
514def readRecord(file,recNum,recSize):
515    file.seek(recNum*recSize)
516    record = file.read(recSize)
517    return record
518
519def readField(record,colTypes,fieldNum):
520    # fieldNum is zero based
521    # record is a string containing the record
522    # colTypes is the types for each of the columns in the record
523    
524    offset = 0
525    for i in range(fieldNum):
526        colType = colTypes[i]
527        
528        if colType == "int":
529            offset+=10
530        elif colType[:4] == "char":
531            size = int(colType[4:])
532            offset += size
533        elif colType == "float":
534            offset+=20
535        elif colType == "datetime":
536            offset+=24
537            
538    colType = colTypes[fieldNum]
539   
540    if colType == "int":
541        value = record[offset:offset+10].strip()
542        if value == "null":
543            val = None
544        else:
545            val = int(value)
546    elif colType == "float":
547        value = record[offset:offset+20].strip()
548        if value == "null":
549            val = None
550        else:        
551            val = float(value)
552    elif colType[:4] == "char":
553        size = int(colType[4:])
554        value = record[offset:offset+size].strip()
555        if value == "null":
556            val = None
557        else:        
558            val = value[1:-1] # remove the ' and ' from each end of the string
559            if type(val) == bytes:
560                val = val.decode("utf-8")            
561    elif colType == "datetime":
562        value = record[offset:offset+24].strip()
563        if value == "null":
564            val = None
565        else:        
566            if type(val) == bytes:
567                val = val.decode("utf-8") 
568            val = datetime.datetime.strptime(val,'%m/%d/%Y %I:%M:%S %p')
569    else:
570        print("Unrecognized Type")
571        raise Exception("Unrecognized Type") 
572    
573    return val
574
575class Item:
576    def __init__(self,key,value):
577        self.key = key
578        self.value = value
579    
580    def __repr__(self):
581        return "Item("+repr(self.key)+","+repr(self.value)+")"
582        
583    def __eq__(self,other):
584        if type(self) != type(other):
585            return False
586        
587        return self.key == other.key
588    
589    def __lt__(self,other):
590        return self.key < other.key
591    
592    def __gt__(self,other):
593        return self.key > other.key
594    
595    def __ge__(self,other):
596        return self.key >= other.key
597    
598    def getValue(self):
599        return self.value
600    
601    def getKey(self):
602        return self.key   
603
604def main():
605    # Select Feed.FeedNum, Feed.Name, FeedAttribType.Name, FeedAttribute.Value where
606    # Feed.FeedID = FeedAttribute.FeedID and FeedAttribute.FeedAtribTypeID = FeedAttribType.ID
607    attribTypeCols = ["int","char20","char60","int","int","int","int"]
608    feedCols = ["int","int","int","char50","datetime","float","float","int","char50","int"]
609    feedAttributeCols = ["int","int","float"]
610    
611    feedAttributeTable = open("FeedAttribute.tbl","r")
612    
613    if os.path.isfile("Feed.idx"):
614        indexFile = open("Feed.idx","r")
615        feedTableRecLength = int(indexFile.readline())
616        feedIndex = eval("".join(indexFile.readlines()))
617    else:
618        feedIndex = BTree(3)
619        feedTable = open("Feed.tbl","r")
620        offset = 0
621        for record in feedTable:
622            feedID = readField(record,feedCols,0)
623            anItem = Item(feedID,offset)
624            feedIndex.insert(anItem)            
625            offset+=1
626            feedTableRecLength = len(record)
627         
628        print("Feed Table Index Created")  
629        indexFile = open("Feed.idx","w")
630        indexFile.write(str(feedTableRecLength)+"\n")
631        indexFile.write(repr(feedIndex)+"\n")
632        indexFile.close()
633        
634    if os.path.isfile("FeedAttribType.idx"):
635        indexFile = open("FeedAttribType.idx","r")
636        attribTypeTableRecLength = int(indexFile.readline())
637        attribTypeIndex = eval("".join(indexFile.readlines()))
638    else:
639        attribTypeIndex = BTree(3)
640        attribTable = open("FeedAttribType.tbl","r")
641        offset = 0
642        for record in attribTable:
643            feedAttribTypeID = readField(record,attribTypeCols,0)
644            anItem = Item(feedAttribTypeID,offset)
645            attribTypeIndex.insert(anItem)
646            offset+=1
647            attribTypeTableRecLength = len(record)
648         
649        print("Attrib Type Table Index Created")
650        indexFile = open("FeedAttribType.idx","w")
651        indexFile.write(str(attribTypeTableRecLength)+"\n")
652        indexFile.write(repr(attribTypeIndex)+"\n")
653        indexFile.close()
654    
655    feedTable = open("Feed.tbl","rb")
656    feedAttribTypeTable = open("FeedAttribType.tbl", "rb")
657    before = datetime.datetime.now()
658    for record in feedAttributeTable:
659        
660        feedID = readField(record,feedAttributeCols,0)
661        feedAttribTypeID = readField(record,feedAttributeCols,1)
662        value = readField(record,feedAttributeCols,2)
663          
664        lookupItem = Item(feedID,None)
665        item = feedIndex.retrieve(lookupItem)
666        offset = item.getValue()
667        feedRecord = readRecord(feedTable,offset,feedTableRecLength)   
668        feedNum = readField(feedRecord,feedCols,2)
669        feedName = readField(feedRecord,feedCols,3)
670        
671        lookupItem = Item(feedAttribTypeID,None)
672        item = attribTypeIndex.retrieve(lookupItem)
673        offset = item.getValue()
674        feedAttribTypeRecord = readRecord(feedAttribTypeTable,offset,attribTypeTableRecLength)
675        feedAttribTypeName = readField(feedAttribTypeRecord,attribTypeCols,1)
676        
677        print(feedNum,feedName,feedAttribTypeName,value)
678    after = datetime.datetime.now()
679    deltaT = after - before
680    milliseconds = deltaT.total_seconds() * 1000    
681    print("Done. The total time for the query without indexing was",milliseconds, \
682      "milliseconds.")
683    
684if __name__ == "__main__":
685    btreemain()

11.3.2. Recursive B-Tree¶

This shell is provided as an implementation that supports a recursive implementation of insert, delete, and update. The starting shell can be downloaded here. As stated above, the program contains two main functions for testing of the B-Tree implementation. The Queue implementation is required for this program and can be downloaded here. This file must be placed in the same directory as the database tables and the B-Tree implementation file.

  1'''
  2  File: btree.py
  3  Author: Kent D. Lee and Steve Hubbard
  4  Date: 06/30/2014
  5  Description: This module provides the BTree class, based on support from
  6    the BTreeNode class.  The BTreeNode class is also implemented in this 
  7    module. This module is meant to support the recursive implementation of 
  8    insert, lookup, and delete within a BTree. 
  9
 10    The module requires the Queue class in the queue module.
 11
 12    This program has two main functions, the btreemain function and the main
 13    function. The btreemain function tests the BTree datatype. The expected
 14    output is provided in a comment after the function. Once the btreemain 
 15    function runs and produces the proper output, the main function can be 
 16    run to test the BTree with the join functionality. 
 17
 18    The main function either builds a new BTree or reads an existing BTree 
 19    from the index files, Feed.idx and FeedAttribType.idx files. If the idx
 20    file does not exist, then a new BTree is built and written to the 
 21    corresponding idx file.
 22'''
 23import datetime
 24import os
 25from copy import deepcopy
 26import sys
 27import queue
 28
 29class BTreeNode:
 30    '''
 31      This class will be used by the BTree class.  Much of the functionality of
 32      BTrees is provided by this class.
 33    '''
 34    def __init__(self, degree = 1, numberOfKeys = 0, items = None, child = None, \
 35        index = None):
 36        ''' Create an empty node with the indicated degree'''
 37        self.numberOfKeys = numberOfKeys
 38        if items != None:
 39            self.items = items
 40        else:
 41            self.items = [None]*2*degree
 42        if child != None:
 43            self.child = child
 44        else:
 45            self.child = [None]*(2*degree+1)
 46        self.index = index
 47
 48    def __repr__(self):
 49        ''' This provides a way of writing a BTreeNode that can be
 50            evaluated to reconstruct the node.
 51        '''
 52        return "BTreeNode("+str(len(self.items)//2)+","+str(self.numberOfKeys)+ \
 53            ","+repr(self.items)+","+repr(self.child)+","+str(self.index)+")\n"
 54
 55    def __str__(self):
 56        st = 'The contents of the node with index '+ \
 57             str(self.index) + ':\n'
 58        for i in range(0, self.numberOfKeys):
 59            st += '   Index   ' + str(i) + '  >  child: '
 60            st += str(self.child[i])
 61            st += '   item: '
 62            st += str(self.items[i]) + '\n'
 63        st += '                 child: '
 64        st += str(self.child[self.numberOfKeys]) + '\n'
 65        return st
 66    
 67    def insert(self,bTree,item):
 68        '''
 69        Insert an item in the node. Return three values as a tuple, 
 70        (left,item,right). If the item fits in the current node, then 
 71        return self as left and None for item and right. Otherwise, return 
 72        two new nodes and the item that will separate the two nodes in the parent. 
 73        '''
 74        pass
 75
 76    def splitNode(self,bTree,item,right):
 77        '''
 78        This method is given the item to insert into this node and the node 
 79        that is to be to the right of the new item once this node is split.
 80        
 81        Return the indices of the two nodes and a key with the item added to 
 82        one of the new nodes. The item is inserted into one of these two 
 83        nodes and not inserted into its children.
 84        '''
 85        pass
 86    
 87    def getLeftMost(self,bTree):
 88        ''' Return the left-most item in the 
 89            subtree rooted at self.
 90        '''
 91        if self.child[0] == None:
 92            return self.items[0]
 93        
 94        return bTree.nodes[self.child[0]].getLeftMost(bTree)
 95
 96    def delete(self,bTree,item):
 97        '''
 98           The delete method returns None if the item is not found
 99           and a deep copy of the item in the tree if it is found.
100           As a side-effect, the tree is updated to delete the item.
101        '''
102        pass
103        
104    def redistributeOrCoalesce(self,bTree,childIndex):
105        '''
106          This method is given a node and a childIndex within 
107          that node that may need redistribution or coalescing.
108          The child needs redistribution or coalescing if the
109          number of keys in the child has fallen below the 
110          degree of the BTree. If so, then redistribution may
111          be possible if the child is a leaf and a sibling has 
112          extra items. If redistribution does not work, then 
113          the child must be coalesced with either the left 
114          or right sibling.
115
116          This method does not return anything, but has the 
117          side-effect of redistributing or coalescing
118          the child node with a sibling if needed. 
119        '''
120        pass 
121
122
123    def getChild(self,i):
124        # Answer the index of the ith child
125        if (0 <= i <= self.numberOfKeys):
126            return self.child[i]
127        else:
128            print( 'Error in getChild().' )
129            
130    def setChild(self, i, childIndex):
131        # Set the ith child of the node to childIndex
132        self.child[i] = childIndex 
133
134    def getIndex(self):
135        return self.index
136
137    def setIndex(self, anInteger):
138        self.index = anInteger
139
140    def isFull(self):
141        ''' Answer True if the receiver is full.  If not, return
142          False.
143        '''
144        return (self.numberOfKeys == len(self.items))
145
146    def getNumberOfKeys(self):
147        return self.numberOfKeys
148
149    def setNumberOfKeys(self, anInt ):
150        self.numberOfKeys = anInt
151
152    def clear(self):
153        self.numberOfKeys = 0
154        self.items = [None]*len(self.items)
155        self.child = [None]*len(self.child)
156
157    def search(self, bTree, item):
158        '''Answer a dictionary satisfying: at 'found'
159          either True or False depending upon whether the receiver
160          has a matching item;  at 'nodeIndex' the index of
161          the matching item within the node; at 'fileIndex' the 
162          node's index. nodeIndex and fileIndex are only set if the 
163          item is found in the current node. 
164        '''
165        pass
166
167
168class BTree:
169    def __init__(self, degree, nodes = {}, rootIndex = 1, freeIndex = 2):
170        self.degree = degree
171        
172        if len(nodes) == 0:
173            self.rootNode = BTreeNode(degree)
174            self.nodes = {}
175            self.rootNode.setIndex(rootIndex)
176            self.writeAt(1, self.rootNode)  
177        else:
178            self.nodes = deepcopy(nodes)
179            self.rootNode = self.nodes[rootIndex]
180              
181        self.rootIndex = rootIndex
182        self.freeIndex = freeIndex
183        
184    def __repr__(self):
185        return "BTree("+str(self.degree)+",\n "+repr(self.nodes)+","+ \
186            str(self.rootIndex)+","+str(self.freeIndex)+")"
187
188    def __str__(self):
189        st = '  The degree of the BTree is ' + str(self.degree)+\
190             '.\n'
191        st += '  The index of the root node is ' + \
192              str(self.rootIndex) + '.\n'
193        for x in range(1, self.freeIndex):
194            node = self.readFrom(x)
195            if node.getNumberOfKeys() > 0:
196                st += str(node) 
197        return st
198
199
200    def delete(self, anItem):
201        ''' Answer None if a matching item is not found.  If found,
202          answer the entire item.
203        ''' 
204        pass
205
206    def getFreeIndex(self):
207        # Answer a new index and update freeIndex.  Private
208        self.freeIndex += 1
209        return self.freeIndex - 1
210
211    def getFreeNode(self):
212        #Answer a new BTreeNode with its index set correctly.
213        #Also, update freeIndex.  Private
214        newNode = BTreeNode(self.degree)
215        index = self.getFreeIndex()
216        newNode.setIndex(index)
217        self.writeAt(index,newNode)
218        return newNode
219
220    def inorderOn(self, aFile):
221        '''
222          Print the items of the BTree in inorder on the file 
223          aFile.  aFile is open for writing.
224        '''
225        aFile.write("An inorder traversal of the BTree:\n")
226        self.inorderOnFrom( aFile, self.rootIndex)
227
228    def inorderOnFrom(self, aFile, index):
229        ''' Print the items of the subtree of the BTree, which is
230          rooted at index, in inorder on aFile.
231        '''
232        pass
233
234    def insert(self, anItem):
235        ''' Answer None if the BTree already contains a matching
236          item. If not, insert a deep copy of anItem and answer
237          anItem.
238        '''
239        pass
240
241    def levelByLevel(self, aFile):
242        ''' Print the nodes of the BTree level-by-level on aFile. )
243        '''
244        pass
245
246    def readFrom(self, index):
247        ''' Answer the node at entry index of the btree structure.
248          Later adapt to files
249        '''
250        if self.nodes.__contains__(index):
251            return self.nodes[index]
252        else:
253            return None
254
255    def recycle(self, aNode):
256        # For now, do nothing
257        aNode.clear()
258
259    def retrieve(self, anItem):
260        ''' If found, answer a deep copy of the matching item.
261          If not found, answer None
262        '''
263        pass
264
265    def __searchTree(self, anItem):
266        ''' Answer a dictionary.  If there is a matching item, at
267          'found' is True, at 'fileIndex' is the index of the node
268          in the BTree with the matching item, and at 'nodeIndex'
269          is the index into the node of the matching item.  If not,
270          at 'found' is False, but the entry for 'fileIndex' is the
271          leaf node where the search terminated.
272        '''
273        pass
274
275 
276    def update(self, anItem):
277        ''' If found, update the item with a matching key to be a
278          deep copy of anItem and answer anItem.  If not, answer None.
279        '''
280        pass
281
282    def writeAt(self, index, aNode):
283        ''' Set the element in the btree with the given index
284          to aNode.  This method must be invoked to make any
285          permanent changes to the btree.  We may later change
286          this method to work with files.
287          This method is complete at this time.
288        '''
289        self.nodes[index] = aNode
290
291def btreemain():
292    print("My/Our name(s) is/are ")
293
294    lst = [10,8,22,14,12,18,2,50,15]
295    
296    b = BTree(2)
297    
298    for x in lst:
299        print(repr(b))
300        print("***Inserting",x)
301        b.insert(x)
302    
303    print(repr(b))
304    
305    lst = [14,50,8,12,18,2,10,22,15]
306    
307    for x in lst:
308        print("***Deleting",x)
309        b.delete(x) 
310        print(repr(b))
311    
312    #return 
313    lst = [54,76]
314    
315    for x in lst:
316        print("***Deleting",x)
317        b.delete(x)
318        print(repr(b))
319        
320    print("***Inserting 14")
321    b.insert(14)
322    
323    print(repr(b))
324    
325    print("***Deleting 2")
326    b.delete(2)
327    
328    print(repr(b))
329    
330    print ("***Deleting 84")
331    b.delete(84)
332    
333    print(repr(b))
334

493, 2: BTreeNode(2,1,[22, 22, 22, 22],[None, None, None, None, None],2)
494, 3: BTreeNode(2,0,[15, 18, None, None],[1, 2, 4, None, None],3)
495, 4: BTreeNode(2,1,[22, 50, None, None],[None, None, None, None, None],4)
496},1,5)
497'''
498
499def readRecord(file,recNum,recSize):
500    file.seek(recNum*recSize)
501    record = file.read(recSize)
502    return record
503
504def readField(record,colTypes,fieldNum):
505    # fieldNum is zero based
506    # record is a string containing the record
507    # colTypes is the types for each of the columns in the record
508    
509    offset = 0
510    for i in range(fieldNum):
511        colType = colTypes[i]
512        
513        if colType == "int":
514            offset+=10
515        elif colType[:4] == "char":
516            size = int(colType[4:])
517            offset += size
518        elif colType == "float":
519            offset+=20
520        elif colType == "datetime":
521            offset+=24
522
523    colType = colTypes[fieldNum]
524
525    if colType == "int":
526        value = record[offset:offset+10].strip()
527        if value == "null":
528            val = None
529        else:
530            val = int(value)
531    elif colType == "float":
532        value = record[offset:offset+20].strip()
533        if value == "null":
534            val = None
535        else:        
536            val = float(value)
537    elif colType[:4] == "char":
538        size = int(colType[4:])
539        value = record[offset:offset+size].strip()
540        if value == "null":
541            val = None
542        else:        
543            val = value[1:-1] # remove the ' and ' from each end of the string
544            if type(val) == bytes:
545                val = val.decode("utf-8") 
546    elif colType == "datetime":
547        value = record[offset:offset+24].strip()
548        if value == "null":
549            val = None
550        else:        
551            if type(val) == bytes:
552                val = val.decode("utf-8") 
553            val = datetime.datetime.strptime(val,'%m/%d/%Y %I:%M:%S %p')
554    else:
555        print("Unrecognized Type")
556        raise Exception("Unrecognized Type") 
557    
558    return val
559
560class Item:
561    def __init__(self,key,value):
562        self.key = key
563        self.value = value
564    
565    def __repr__(self):
566        return "Item("+repr(self.key)+","+repr(self.value)+")"
567
568    def __eq__(self,other):
569        if type(self) != type(other):
570            return False
571
572        return self.key == other.key
573    
574    def __lt__(self,other):
575        return self.key < other.key
576    
577    def __gt__(self,other):
578        return self.key > other.key
579    
580    def __ge__(self,other):
581        return self.key >= other.key
582    
583    def getValue(self):
584        return self.value
585    
586    def getKey(self):
587        return self.key
588            
589
590def main():
591    # Select Feed.FeedNum, Feed.Name, FeedAttribType.Name, FeedAttribute.Value where
592    # Feed.FeedID = FeedAttribute.FeedID and FeedAttribute.FeedAtribTypeID = FeedAttribType.ID
593    attribTypeCols = ["int","char20","char60","int","int","int","int"]
594    feedCols = ["int","int","int","char50","datetime","float","float","int","char50","int"]
595    feedAttributeCols = ["int","int","float"]
596    
597    feedAttributeTable = open("FeedAttribute.tbl","r")
598    
599    if os.path.isfile("Feed.idx"):
600        indexFile = open("Feed.idx","r")
601        feedTableRecLength = int(indexFile.readline())
602        feedIndex = eval("".join(indexFile.readlines()))
603    else:
604        feedIndex = BTree(3)
605        feedTable = open("Feed.tbl","r")
606        offset = 0
607        for record in feedTable:
608            feedID = readField(record,feedCols,0)
609            anItem = Item(feedID,offset)
610            feedIndex.insert(anItem)
611            offset+=1
612            feedTableRecLength = len(record)
613         
614        print("Feed Table Index Created")  
615        indexFile = open("Feed.idx","w")
616        indexFile.write(str(feedTableRecLength)+"\n")
617        indexFile.write(repr(feedIndex)+"\n")
618        indexFile.close()
619        
620    if os.path.isfile("FeedAttribType.idx"):
621        indexFile = open("FeedAttribType.idx","r")
622        attribTypeTableRecLength = int(indexFile.readline())
623        attribTypeIndex = eval("".join(indexFile.readlines()))
624    else:
625        attribTypeIndex = BTree(3)
626        attribTable = open("FeedAttribType.tbl","r")
627        offset = 0
628        for record in attribTable:
629            feedAttribTypeID = readField(record,attribTypeCols,0)
630            anItem = Item(feedAttribTypeID,offset)
631            attribTypeIndex.insert(anItem)
632            offset+=1
633            attribTypeTableRecLength = len(record)
634         
635        print("Attrib Type Table Index Created")
636        indexFile = open("FeedAttribType.idx","w")
637        indexFile.write(str(attribTypeTableRecLength)+"\n")
638        indexFile.write(repr(attribTypeIndex)+"\n")
639        indexFile.close()
640    
641    feedTable = open("Feed.tbl","rb")
642    feedAttribTypeTable = open("FeedAttribType.tbl", "rb")
643    before = datetime.datetime.now()
644    for record in feedAttributeTable:
645        
646        feedID = readField(record,feedAttributeCols,0)
647        feedAttribTypeID = readField(record,feedAttributeCols,1)
648        value = readField(record,feedAttributeCols,2)
649          
650        lookupItem = Item(feedID,None)
651        item = feedIndex.retrieve(lookupItem)
652        offset = item.getValue()
653        feedRecord = readRecord(feedTable,offset,feedTableRecLength)   
654        feedNum = readField(feedRecord,feedCols,2)
655        feedName = readField(feedRecord,feedCols,3)
656        
657        lookupItem = Item(feedAttribTypeID,None)
658        item = attribTypeIndex.retrieve(lookupItem)
659        offset = item.getValue()
660        feedAttribTypeRecord = readRecord(feedAttribTypeTable,offset, \
661            attribTypeTableRecLength)               
662        feedAttribTypeName = readField(feedAttribTypeRecord,attribTypeCols,1)
663        
664        print(feedNum,feedName,feedAttribTypeName,value)
665    after = datetime.datetime.now()
666    deltaT = after - before
667    milliseconds = deltaT.total_seconds() * 1000    
668    print("Done. The total time for the query with indexing was",milliseconds, \
669        "milliseconds.")
670    
671if __name__ == "__main__":
672    main()
673
